getUsers({ cache: Cache.Long })

const Cache = {
  Long: 3600,
  Short: 60,
  No: null,
}

function request({method, url, body, cache }) {
  const data = localStorage.has(`${method}-${url}`)
  if (!data) {
    return axios.get({ method, url, body })
      .then(data => {
        localStorage.set(`${method}-${url}`, JSON.stringify({ date: new Date(), data })
        return data
      })
  }
}
